Strategy Logic

  • Contract Rollover: Auto-rollover 5 days before expiry
  • Product Switch: Based on direction signal strength x product beta
  • Near/Far Switch: Z-score > 1.0σ → Far | Z-score < 0.3σ → Near
  • Cooldown: 6 bars between switches
